*Q1.* 🐜 Which is the SMALLEST? 1, 75, 53, 48
A) 53
B) 48
C) 1
D) 75
✅ *Answer:* C) 1
💡 1 is the smallest.
━━━━━━━━━━
*Q2.* 🔢 In ascending order, which number comes in the MIDDLE? 83, 79, 26
A) 26
B) 80
C) 79
D) 83
✅ *Answer:* C) 79
💡 Sorted: 26, 79, 83; middle is 79.

A) 84
B) 85
C) 83
D) 82
✅ *Answer:* A) 84
💡 Adding 2 each time, next is 84.

*Q1025.* 🎈 Kabir had 15 flowers but 13 flew away. How many flowers left?
A) 3
B) 1
C) 2
D) 15
✅ *Answer:* C) 2
💡 15 - 13 = 2 flowers left.

💡 1 less than 60 is 59.
━━━━━━━━━━
*Q5810.* 📉 Arranged greatest → smallest, which comes FIRST? 100, 32, 22
A) 22
B) 100
C) 32
D) 101
✅ *Answer:* B) 100
💡 Descending order starts with 100.
━━━━━━━━━━
*Q5811.* 🔎 Which is GREATER: 30 or 41?
A) 30
B) 29
C) 11
D) 41
✅ *Answer:* D) 41
💡 41 is greater than 30.

*Q5812.* 🐜 Which is the SMALLEST? 41, 4, 38, 34

B) 38

D) 4
✅ *Answer:* D) 4
💡 4 is the smallest.
